line=1262 tag=T:      because, true, we are really in freedom,
line=1263 tag=T:      but, if God wants, it may be,
line=1264 tag=B:
line=1265 tag=B:       13
line=1266 tag=M:           The particle ma' is the common form of negation in Yucatec Maya. It can either be used with a
line=1267 tag=M:  verb or a lexical phrase, or alone (just to say "no"). Ma' usually precedes modal or aspectual prefixes; but
line=1268 tag=M:  some aspectual prefixes (like k-) cannot appear with it, and in this case ma' directly precedes the ergative
line=1269 tag=M:  pronoun.
line=1270 tag=B:        14
line=1271 tag=M:           For the completive "never" (something that has never happened, but not that will never happen),
line=1272 tag=M:  the form mix jun tèen/ mix jum p'ùul ("nor one time") is used.
line=1273 tag=B:
line=1274 tag=M:  28 / Institut für Ethnologie der Universität Bern: Arbeitsblätter Nr. 14, 1996
line=1275 tag=B:
line=1276 tag=T:       but not very soon,
line=1277 tag=T:       right now,
line=1278 tag=T:       I say that there won't be any revolt soon,
line=1279 tag=T:       maybe (it is sure that it will happen) one day,
line=1280 tag=T:       but we don't know really in what time".[TI.1]

line=1630 tag=T:       no matter, fathers,

line=1637 tag=T:       now, it is finished,
line=1638 tag=T:       nobody now will go to do his service"18
line=1639 tag=T:       And then they were told:
line=1640 tag=T:       "Now everything is finished
line=1641 tag=T:       (one day) maybe it will happen again,
line=1642 tag=T:       but not soon,
line=1643 tag=T:       (one day) you will be called to account again,
line=1644 tag=T:       but that, nobody knows who will do it,
line=1645 tag=T:       [thus,] the great people know how will come the truth" [CVI.12]

line=854 tag=M:           Alternatively, the verb p'áat `leave', `abandon' might be used instead of bin. The source of p'áat
line=855 tag=M:  can be specified by an adjunct, but p'áat is far less frequent in narratives. Notice, though, that (28) is a
line=856 tag=M:  constructed example and that I'm not entirely sure how native speaker would translate (27) out of
line=857 tag=M:  context.
